 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99</B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Dec. 20, 2022 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>General Mills Reports Fiscal
2023 Second-quarter Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>and Raises Full-year Outlook </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> were up 11&nbsp;percent </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

levels; adjusted operating profit was up 7&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Diluted earnings per share (EPS) of $1.01 increased 4&nbsp;percent from the prior year; adjusted diluted EPS
of $1.10 was up 12&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Company raises full-year fiscal 2023 outlook </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&sup1;</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><I>Please see Note 8 to the Consolidated Financial Statements below for reconciliation of this and other <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures used in this release. </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">MINNEAPOLIS (Dec. 20, 2022) &#150;
General Mills, Inc. (NYSE: GIS) today reported results for its fiscal 2023 second quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We continued to execute well and
delivered strong top and bottom-line growth in the second quarter,&#148; said General Mills Chairman and Chief Executive Officer Jeff Harmening. &#147;Amid ongoing volatility in the operating environment, we remain focused on driving our Accelerate
strategy by investing in brand building and innovation, strengthening our capabilities, and continuing to reshape our portfolio. With strong first-half results and positive momentum on our business, we are increasing our full-year outlook for
organic net sales, adjusted operating profit, and adjusted diluted EPS growth.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills is executing its Accelerate strategy
to drive sustainable, profitable growth and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-tier</FONT> shareholder returns over the long term. The strategy focuses on four pillars to create competitive advantages and win: boldly building brands, relentlessly
innovating, unleashing scale, and standing for good. The company is prioritizing its core markets, global platforms, and local gem brands that have the best prospects for profitable growth and is committed to reshaping its portfolio with strategic
acquisitions and divestitures to further enhance its growth profile. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Second Quarter Results Summary </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> increased 4&nbsp;percent to $5.2&nbsp;billion, including a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5-point</FONT> headwind from net divestiture and acquisition activity and 1 point of unfavorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales increased 11&nbsp;percent, driven by positive organic net price
realization and mix, partially offset by lower organic pound volume. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was up 20 basis points to 32.7&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by favorable net price
realization and mix, partially offset by higher input costs and unfavorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects. Adjusted gross margin was up 100 basis points to 33.2&nbsp;percent of
net sales, driven by favorable net price realization and mix and Holistic Margin Management (HMM) cost savings, partially offset by input cost inflation, higher other cost of goods sold, and supply chain deleverage. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $800&nbsp;million essentially matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
levels, reflecting higher gross profit dollars offset by higher selling, general, and administrative (SG&amp;A) expenses. <B>Operating profit margin</B> of 15.3&nbsp;percent was down 60 basis points. Constant-currency adjusted operating profit
increased 7&nbsp;percent, driven by higher adjusted gross profit dollars, partially offset by higher adjusted SG&amp;A expenses. Adjusted operating profit margin increased 60 basis points to 16.9&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> increased 1&nbsp;percent to $606&nbsp;million and <B>diluted
EPS</B> was up 4&nbsp;percent to $1.01, driven by lower net shares outstanding and a lower effective tax rate, partially offset by lower benefit plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income. Adjusted diluted EPS of $1.10 increased
12&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by higher adjusted operating profit, a lower adjusted effective tax rate, and lower net shares outstanding, partially offset by lower benefit plan
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Six Month Results Summary </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> increased 4&nbsp;percent to $9.9&nbsp;billion, including a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5-point</FONT> headwind from net divestiture and acquisition activity and 1 point of unfavorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales increased 11&nbsp;percent, driven by positive organic net price
realization and mix, partially offset by lower organic pound volume. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was down 210 basis points to 31.7&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by higher input costs,
unfavorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects, and the impact of market index pricing on bakery flour, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. Adjusted gross
margin was up 60 basis points to 34.0&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by higher input costs and the impact of market index pricing on bakery flour. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $1.9&nbsp;billion was up 15&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by net gains on
divestitures, partially offset by lower gross profit dollars, unfavorable net corporate investment activity, and higher SG&amp;A expenses.<B> Operating profit margin</B> of 19.0&nbsp;percent was up 180 basis points. Constant-currency adjusted
operating profit increased 8&nbsp;percent, driven by higher adjusted gross profit dollars, partially offset by higher adjusted SG&amp;A expenses. Adjusted operating profit margin increased 50 basis points to 17.7&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> increased 16&nbsp;percent to $1.4&nbsp;billion and <B>diluted
EPS</B> was up 19&nbsp;percent to $2.36, primarily reflecting higher operating profit and lower net shares outstanding. Adjusted diluted EPS of $2.21 was up 13&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by higher adjusted operating profit,
a lower adjusted effective tax rate, and lower net shares outstanding. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Notes on Comparability </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Financial results in the first half of fiscal 2023 reflected the acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treat business in the first quarter of fiscal 2022; the
divestiture of the European yogurt business in the third quarter of fiscal 2022; the divestiture of certain international dough businesses in the third and fourth quarters of fiscal 2022; the acquisition of the TNT Crust foodservice business in the
first quarter of fiscal 2023; and the divestiture of the Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in the first quarter of fiscal 2023. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First-half results in fiscal 2023 also included the impact of a voluntary recall on certain international
<I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream products, which was a headwind to net sales and operating profit results in the International segment. Unallocated corporate items in the first half included an additional
$24&nbsp;million of charges related to product disposals associated with the ice cream recall that were excluded from adjusted operating profit results. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">

fiscal 2023. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Operating Segment Results </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Note:

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Retail Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second-quarter net sales for General Mills&#146; North America Retail segment increased 11&nbsp;percent to $3.4&nbsp;billion, driven by favorable net price
realization and mix, partially offset by lower pound volume and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-point</FONT> headwind from the Helper and Suddenly Salad divestiture. Organic net sales increased 13&nbsp;percent. Net sales increased
18&nbsp;percent in U.S. Snacks, 10&nbsp;percent in U.S. Meals&nbsp;&amp; Baking Solutions, and 10&nbsp;percent in U.S. Morning Foods. Constant-currency net sales were up 4&nbsp;percent in Canada. Segment operating profit of $837&nbsp;million was up
24&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant currency, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix and HMM cost savings, partially offset by input cost inflation, lower volume, and higher SG&amp;A expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through six months, North America Retail segment net sales increased 11&nbsp;percent to $6.4&nbsp;billion, including a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-point</FONT> headwind from the Helper and Suddenly Salad divestiture. Organic net sales were up 13&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit of $1.6&nbsp;billion was up 22&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant currency,
driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by higher input costs, lower volume, and higher SG&amp;A expenses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Pet
Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second-quarter net sales for the Pet segment essentially matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> levels at $593&nbsp;million,
with favorable net price realization and mix offset by lower pound volume. Organic net sales were flat. Net sales performance was negatively impacted by a reduction in retailer inventory, with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">all-channel</FONT>
retail sales up high single digits in the quarter. Excluding the retailer inventory change, net sales results were broadly in line with company expectations and reflected continued strength of the Blue Buffalo brand, partially offset by a short-term
headwind from capacity constraints and related customer service challenges. Pet net sales performance is expected to accelerate in the second half of fiscal 2023 due to increased capacity, improved customer service, increased brand-building
investment, and an expectation for stable retailer inventory levels. Segment operating profit totaled $87&nbsp;million compared to $132&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by high-teens input cost inflation, a significant increase in costs
related to capacity expansion and supply chain disruptions, and lower volume, including the impact of the retailer inventory reduction. These headwinds were partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through six months, Pet segment net sales increased 8&nbsp;percent to $1.2&nbsp;billion, including a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-point</FONT> benefit from the pet treats acquisition. Organic net sales were up 6&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit was down 15&nbsp;percent to $210&nbsp;million, driven primarily by higher input costs, lower
volume, and higher SG&amp;A expenses, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Foodservice Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second-quarter net sales for the North America Foodservice segment increased 24&nbsp;percent to $583&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price realization
and mix, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5-point</FONT> benefit from market index pricing on bakery flour. Net sales results also included a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">6-point</FONT> benefit from the TNT Crust acquisition. Organic
net sales were up 17&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit increased 20&nbsp;percent to $82&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by higher input costs and higher SG&amp;A expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through six months, North America Foodservice net sales increased 22&nbsp;percent to $1.1&nbsp;billion, including a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5-point</FONT> benefit from the TNT Crust acquisition. Organic net sales were up 17&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit was down 3&nbsp;percent to $135&nbsp;million, driven by higher input costs and higher SG&amp;A
expenses, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>International Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second-quarter net sales for the International segment were down 27&nbsp;percent to $672&nbsp;million, driven by lower pound volume, including the impact of
yogurt and dough divestitures and the ice cream recall, and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">6-point</FONT> headwind from foreign currency exchange, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were up
5&nbsp;percent, with growth in Brazil, distributor markets, and Europe&nbsp;&amp; Australia, partially offset by a decline in China due to continued consumer mobility restrictions as well as the impact of the international ice cream recall. Segment
operating profit totaled $18&nbsp;million compared to $59&nbsp;million a year ago, driven by higher input costs and lower volume, including the impacts of the yogurt and dough divestitures and the ice cream recall, partially offset by favorable net
price realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through six months, International net sales were down 28&nbsp;percent to
$1.3&nbsp;billion, driven by lower pound volume, including the impact of yogurt and dough divestitures and the ice cream recall, and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">6-point</FONT> headwind from foreign currency exchange, partially offset by
favorable net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were up 1&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit totaled $53&nbsp;million compared to $120&nbsp;million a year ago, driven by lower volume, including the impacts of the yogurt and dough
divestitures and the ice cream recall, and higher input costs, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Joint Venture Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second-quarter net sales
for Cereal Partners Worldwide (CPW) increased 2&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven by positive net price realization and mix, partially offset by lower volume. Constant-currency net sales for
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT> Japan (HDJ) were down 10&nbsp;percent as the business lapped strong new product performance a year ago. Combined <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures
totaled $25&nbsp;million compared to $33&nbsp;million a year ago, driven by unfavorable foreign currency exchange as well as lower constant-currency profit at HDJ, partially offset by positive price/mix at CPW. Through six months, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures totaled $45&nbsp;million compared to $62&nbsp;million a year ago. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Other
Income Statement Items </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unallocated corporate items totaled $212&nbsp;million net expense in the second quarter of fiscal 2023, compared to
$132&nbsp;million net expense a year ago. Excluding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation effects and other items affecting comparability, unallocated corporate items totaled
$142&nbsp;million net expense this year compared to $112&nbsp;million net expense last year, driven primarily by increased capability investments and certain discrete favorable items a year ago. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring, impairment, and other exit costs totaled $11&nbsp;million compared to $2&nbsp;million a year ago <I>(please see Note 4 below
for more information on these charges)</I>. Benefit plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income totaled $22&nbsp;million in the second quarter compared to $28&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by an increase in interest
cost, partially offset by lower amortization of losses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net interest expense of $92&nbsp;million was down 1&nbsp;percent, driven
primarily by lower average long-term debt balances, partially offset by higher rates. The effective tax rate in the quarter was 20.2&nbsp;percent compared to 21.7&nbsp;percent last year <I>(please see Note 7 below for more information on our
effective tax rate)</I>. The adjusted effective tax rate was 21.1&nbsp;percent compared to 22.3&nbsp;percent a year ago. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net earnings attributable to redeemable and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-controlling</FONT> interests totaled $2&nbsp;million in the quarter compared to $11&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by the sale of the company&#146;s interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and
Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl in fiscal 2022. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Cash Flow Generation and Cash Returns </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash provided by operating activities totaled $1.2&nbsp;billion through six months of fiscal 2023 compared to $1.5&nbsp;billion a year ago, driven by an
increase in inventory and higher cash tax payments. Capital investments of $227&nbsp;million were up 1&nbsp;percent from a year ago. Dividends paid increased 4&nbsp;percent to $648&nbsp;million. General Mills repurchased approximately
12.1&nbsp;million shares of common stock through six months of fiscal 2023 for a total of $901&nbsp;million compared to $375&nbsp;million in share repurchases a year ago. Average diluted shares outstanding in the first half decreased 2&nbsp;percent
to 604&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fiscal 2023 Outlook </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills continues to expect the largest factors impacting its performance in fiscal 2023 will be the economic health of consumers, the inflationary cost
environment, and the frequency and severity of disruptions in the supply chain. Relative to its previous outlook, the company now expects to generate stronger organic net sales growth through better volume performance and improved price/mix. Volume
elasticities in the second half of fiscal 2023 are expected to remain below historical levels. For the full year, the company expects input cost inflation of 14 to 15&nbsp;percent of total cost of goods sold, HMM cost savings of 3 to 4&nbsp;percent
of cost of goods sold, moderately lower supply chain disruptions compared to the prior year, and increased investment in brand building and other growth-driving activities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company&#146;s updated full-year fiscal 2023 financial targets are summarized below: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

of 6 to 7&nbsp;percent growth. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

to the previous range of between flat and up 3&nbsp;percent in constant currency. Both the current and previous ranges include a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> net headwind from divestitures and acquisitions and an estimated <FONT

previous range of up 2 to 5&nbsp;percent in constant currency. The updated outlook reflects stronger adjusted operating profit growth and higher net interest expense due to increasing rates. Both the current and previous ranges include a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> net headwind from divestitures and acquisitions and an estimated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> headwind from the ice cream recall. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">GENERAL MILLS, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTES TO CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(Unaudited) </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The accompanying Consolidated Financial Statements of General Mills, Inc. (we, us, our, General Mills, or the
Company) have been prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States for annual and interim financial information. In the opinion of management, all adjustments considered necessary for a fair presentation
have been included and are of a normal recurring nature. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(2)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In the third quarter of fiscal 2022, we completed a new organization structure to streamline our global
operations. This global reorganization required us to reevaluate our operating segments. Under our new organization structure, our chief operating decision maker assesses performance and makes decisions about resources to be allocated to our
operating segments as follows: North America Retail; International; Pet; and North America Foodservice. We have restated our net sales by segment and segment operating profit amounts to reflect our new operating segments. These segment changes had
no effect on previously reported consolidated net sales, operating profit, net earnings attributable to General Mills, or earnings per share. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(3)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the first quarter of fiscal 2023, we acquired TNT Crust, a manufacturer of high-quality frozen pizza
crusts for regional and national pizza chains, foodservice distributors, and retail outlets, for a purchase price of $253&nbsp;million. We financed the transaction with U.S. commercial paper. We consolidated the TNT Crust business into our
Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $154&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the North America Foodservice segment and is not deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material. The
consolidated results of the TNT Crust business are reported in our North America Foodservice segment on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-month</FONT> lag. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first quarter of fiscal 2023, we completed the asset sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business to Eagle
Family Foods Group for $607&nbsp;million and recorded a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $442&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During
the first quarter of fiscal 2022, we acquired the pet treats business for $1.2&nbsp;billion in cash. We financed the transaction with a combination of cash on hand and short-term debt. We consolidated the pet treats business into our Consolidated
Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $762&nbsp;million, indefinite-lived intangible assets for the <I>Nudges</I>, <I>Top Chews</I>, and <I>True Chews</I> brands totaling $330&nbsp;million in aggregate, and a finite-lived customer relationship
asset of $40&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the Pet segment and is deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(4)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended November&nbsp;27, 2022, we did not
undertake any new restructuring actions. We recorded $12&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the second quarter of fiscal 2023 and $14&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended
November&nbsp;27, 2022, related to restructuring actions previously announced. We recorded $3&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the second quarter of fiscal 2022 and a $1&nbsp;million net recovery of restructuring charges in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended November&nbsp;28, 2021, related to restructuring actions previously announced. We expect these actions to be completed by the end of fiscal 2024. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(7)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The effective tax rate for the second quarter of fiscal 2023 was 20.2&nbsp;percent compared to
21.7&nbsp;percent for the second quarter of fiscal 2022. The 1.5 percentage point decrease was primarily due to certain nonrecurring discrete tax benefits and favorable changes in earnings mix by jurisdiction in fiscal 2023. Our effective tax rate
excluding certain items affecting comparability was 21.1&nbsp;percent in the second quarter of fiscal 2023, compared to 22.3&nbsp;percent in the same period last year (see the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures&#148;
section below for a description of our use of measures not defined by GAAP). The 1.2 percentage point decrease was primarily due to certain nonrecurring discrete tax benefits and favorable changes in earnings mix by jurisdiction in the second
quarter of fiscal 2023. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The effective tax rate for the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended
November&nbsp;27, 2022, was 20.8&nbsp;percent compared to 21.7&nbsp;percent for the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended November&nbsp;28, 2021. The 0.9 percentage point decrease was primarily due to certain nonrecurring
discrete tax benefits and favorable changes in earnings mix by jurisdiction in fiscal 2023, partially offset by unfavorable tax components related to the divestitures incurred in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended
November&nbsp;27, 2022. Our effective tax rate excluding certain items affecting comparability was 20.4&nbsp;percent in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended November&nbsp;27, 2022, compared to 22.0&nbsp;percent in the
same period last year (see the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures&#148; section below for a description of our use of measures not defined by GAAP). The 1.6 percentage point decrease is primarily due to certain
nonrecurring discrete tax benefits and favorable changes in earnings mix by jurisdiction in fiscal 2023. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(8)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">We have included measures in this release that are not defined by GAAP. We believe that these measures provide
useful information to investors, and include these measures in other communications to investors. For each of these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, we are providing below a reconciliation of the differences
between the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure and the most directly comparable GAAP measure, an explanation of why we believe the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure provides useful information to
investors and any additional material purposes for which our management or Board of Directors uses the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure. These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures should be viewed in
addition to, and not in lieu of, the comparable GAAP measure. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We provide organic net sales growth rates for our
consolidated net sales and segment net sales. This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the Board of Directors&#146; measurement of our performance for incentive compensation purposes.
We believe that organic net sales growth rates provide useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying performance in our net sales by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations,
acquisitions, divestitures, and a 53rd&nbsp;fiscal week, when applicable, have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability. A reconciliation of these measures to reported net sales
growth rates, the relevant GAAP measures, are included in our Operating Segment Results above. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain measures in this release are
presented excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange (constant-currency). To present this information, current period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are translated into United States dollars at
the average exchange rates in effect during the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year, rather than the actual average exchange rates in effect during the current fiscal year. Therefore, the foreign currency impact is equal to current year
results in local currencies multiplied by the change in the average foreign currency exchange rate between the current fiscal period and the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year. We believe that these constant-currency measures provide
useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying performance by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal 2023 outlook for organic net sales growth, adjusted operating profit growth, adjusted diluted EPS growth, and free cash flow
conversion are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures that exclude, or have otherwise been adjusted for, items impacting comparability, including the effect of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, acquisitions,
divestitures, and a 53rd week, when applicable. We are not able to reconcile these forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures to their most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure without
unreasonable efforts because we are unable to predict with a reasonable degree of certainty the actual impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates or the timing of acquisitions and divestitures throughout fiscal 2023. The unavailable
information could have a significant impact on our fiscal 2023 GAAP financial results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For fiscal 2023, we currently expect: foreign
currency exchange rates (based on a blend of forward and forecasted rates and hedge positions) and completed acquisitions and divestitures to reduce net sales growth by approximately 4.5&nbsp;percent; foreign currency exchange rates to reduce
adjusted operating profit and adjusted diluted EPS growth by approximately 1&nbsp;percent; and restructuring charges and project-related costs, transaction and acquisition integration costs related to actions previously announced, and product
disposal charges related to the ice cream recall to total approximately $55&nbsp;million to $60&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Significant Items Impacting
Comparability </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Several measures below are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from infrequently occurring
events or items that, in management&#146;s judgement, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following are descriptions of significant items impacting comparability of our results. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Divestitures gain, net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net divestitures gain primarily related to the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in fiscal 2023. Please see
Note 3. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions
recognized in unallocated corporate items. Please see Note 5. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Investment activity, net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Valuation adjustments and the loss on sale of certain corporate investments in fiscal 2023. Valuation adjustments and the gain on sale of
certain corporate investments in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 5. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Product recall</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Voluntary recall costs recorded in fiscal 2023 related to certain international <I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I>
ice cream products. Please see Note 5. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Restructuring charges (recoveries)</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring charges for previously announced restructuring actions recorded in fiscal 2023 and fiscal 2022. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Acquisition integration costs</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Integration costs primarily resulting from the acquisition of TNT Crust in fiscal 2023. Integration costs resulting from the acquisition of
Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 3. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Transaction costs</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Transaction costs primarily related to the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in fiscal 2023. Transaction
costs related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl and the sale of our European dough businesses in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 3. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-income</FONT> tax recovery</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item recorded in fiscal 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>CPW restructuring charges</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">CPW restructuring charges related to previously announced restructuring actions. </P>
</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Operating Profit Growth on a Constant-currency Basis</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the measurement of our performance for incentive
compensation purposes. We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors because it is the operating profit measure we use to evaluate operating profit performance on a comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. The measure is evaluated on a constant-currency basis by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given the volatility in foreign currency exchange rates. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our adjusted operating
profit growth on a constant-currency basis is calculated as follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Diluted EPS and Related Constant-currency Growth Rates</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management. We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors
because it is the profitability measure we use to evaluate earnings performance on a comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. </P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>

<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">%&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Note: Table may not foot due to rounding. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Effective Income Tax Rate </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We believe this measure provides useful information to investors because it presents the adjusted effective income tax rate on a comparable <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted effective income tax rates are calculated as
follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
